<Review>Despite all the reviews, I decided to take a look at Summer House after unsuccessful attempts in finding affordable rentals in surrounding neighborhoods. I had lived in Alameda before AND took a look at Summer House 3 years prior. Now, I'm a resident here. I have to say that the new management has changed this place for the better. Now that construction is complete, the grounds are gorgeous with water fountains all around, a gigantic swimming pool and beautiful plants and flowers.  The groundskeepers should be given full credit, as I see them outside everyday working on keeping the place clean and attractive (*reviews have been given about the trash and furniture around the dumpsters, which is accurate still, however, this is at the fault of the residents, not the property managers). The ordinary apartments are comparable to their going rates, so if you are looking for something plain to get you through the year, this is a great spot. They come with a double sink, dishwasher, electric stove, microwave, carpeted rooms, and easy cable hookup. So far we've had to call maintenance twice in the 3 months that we've been here. Though some appliances were not working properly when we moved in, the maintenance people were there on time and fixed our problems right away... no questions asked. Be careful for the "water fee" which is divided among the complex as a whole and attached to your monthly rent. There is ample parking but the car gates are not secure. Plenty of kids here who play in the complex when school is out. We live with a 10 year-old so he made friends right away. Last note, it can get a little noisy since the walls are pretty thin. I would suggest sticking with a top floor.<//Review>< username>

It was a bad omen when I went to the bank for a cashier's check for rent and deposit, and the teller told me I should tear it up find a new place if I hadn't signed anything yet.  These have been my negative experiences in the one year I have lived here:

1. My roommate and I voiced concern over parking on the tour.  Our guide said, "The 3 bedroom apartments come with 2 spaces."  This is an outright lie. The excuse: "Oh, sorry, he is new here."

2. We were told the prices of the apartments are all reflected on the website.  We applied for our apartment based on website listing, and then the contract was for $200 more per month.  Their excuse was, "Sometimes there's a significant delay between the website updates and actual rent changes, especially during the summer when there are a lot of moves."

3. After signing a lease for $200 more than expected and one fewer parking space, a new blank lease appeared in our email  a month later asking for even more money.  They said there was an error, and we weren't being charged enough.  They didn't push it after we pointed out this was blatantly illegal, but they still act like they're doing us a huge favor and we're just trying to scheme them out of cash.

4. There is a significant amount of noise at night.  I was particularly peeved one night when a car with a custom engine and very loud after stock muffler was parked below my window at 1:30 AM just revving the engine over and over again.  Then the guy left the doors open on both sides and BLASTED his stereo.  I was going to call security, but when I looked again, I saw that it was the security guard.  I had to be at work 5 hours later.

5. Management is in cahoots with some local towing company, and they call them immediately if anything is amiss.  If you need to unload groceries because you don't have enough parking spots that come with the apartment, you're gambling if it will be there when you return, even if it's only 10 min.

6. People like to dig through the dumpster below my bedroom window on a daily basis, and they can be rather loud at times, too.

7. There are loud children everywhere.  Make sure your apartment isn't next to the parking lot or the playground.

8. You are next to 2 schools, which is convenient if you have kids, but a pain around 8AM and 3PM.

9. There's a creepy old guy in the complex across the street who just walks up and down the sidewalk and calls police for people who are parked illegally, even if you tell him you just need to run a bag of groceries upstairs before you hunt for parking elsewhere.

Basically, I should have listened to my bank teller.  I'm moving in a week, and I can't wait.< /Text>

Went in there with my family looking to dine in. Not only was the restaurant and tables dirty, but the customer service was very unpleasant. Ice machine was not working and fountain drinks were warm. Definitely cannot do a warm soda on hot So-Cal day.

I mentioned to the cashier Valery that she should let the customer know Ice machine is not working or to put up a sign. She completely ignored me. I tried to get a refund for the drinks, but she bartered 2 biscuits instead.

P.S. Chick Fill A chicken sandwich and customer service 1k% better is an understatement</review>

<Review>I'm picking up dinner on a Sunday for the family, 4 big people. My last experience with KFC really left a sour feeling..  so I won't be doing them again any time soon.

So we decided to give the local Popeye's a shot and we were delighted. I walked into a clean well organized place, was met by two wonderful ladies who couldn't wait to assist, one helped me choose the best deals while the other assisted cheerfully.   They were quite the sales people too..  offering all he goodies that I had no idea were there, I had to decline the goodies but I did get a great deal on a 11 piece family meal with extra fixins'.   My items were carefully packed, all the condiments were added to the bags, and the happy faces took me..   was a pleasurable experience.

At home we dug straight in, the Taters, Cole slaw, and Biscuits were excellent, quite a difference from the KFC.. I was expecting different and I got it.  Oh, btw I did get the spicy recipe..   I just love my spices.  The chicken was very good..  again very different than the KFC.  My white meat was a bit dry, I like my beasts plump and juicy, but the flavor was amazing.

Overall I highly recommend this Popeye's and I'll definitely be going back.  Their just a bit east of Laurel Canyon, give 'em a try and say Hi to those sweet ladies for me while your there :)< /Review>< pics>
None</pics>
